<rate>5< /rate>< review>
Pet Choice on MacArthur is my go to shop for all my kitty needs. The owner is incredibly nice, so nice that I always leave the store in a better mood than when I entered. He has random give-always (of good stuff!) and is an excellent source of advice and referrals.
One of my cats has special dietary needs, the brand of cat food isn‚Äôt commonly found at smaller pet stores. I heard through a neighborhood group that the owner will special order pet supplies if requested and that he matches or beats most big-box prices. Turns out, they were right! If I call in my order by mid-day Wednesday I can usually pick up Thursday afternoon.
Prices are as good, if not better, than the big retail chains. I have not used grooming services but have been on site and seen the handling and treatment of animals and feel good fully endorsing this store and it‚Äôs owner. The decor is a little funky but the service is first class. :)<//review>

< Review>
This is the best pet store around. Also a dog grooming service.  The owner Freddie is awesome. If you claim to suppport local business and have a pet this is the best option. The owner Freddie has lived in the Laurel district over 20 years. Most importantly these days is the prices. They Can't Be Beat!!
CHEAPER than Amazon. CHEAPER than PET FOOD EXPRESS and PETCO. Often people go out of they're way for convince and don't even price check or just order off amazon cause "its easier" this place always has some quick parking unlike the rest of MacArthur blvd. I fear that without the local communities support this wonderful local long standing business could go under so to big name stores and people just assuming his little shop will be more expensive. My 50lb bag of taste of the wild is 3.20 cheaper than on Amazon, I used to buy at pet food express before I found Freddie. I was paying 3 dollars and change more. Same with tread and dog grooming accessories. Seems small to us the consumer where we buy dog/cat food etc. but that support is huge to a local bussines owner. I support local business owners.
Mike (Maxwell Park)< /Review>

<Rate>5</Rate>< review>
For the couple who is in empty nest training.. OR just wanting to get away... this is the perfect place to practice!  Clean and beautiful with full growth trees shading the courtyard and a couples tree swing to go with it.  The hosts... alas.. are what we all aspire to in our relationships... they served us a beautifully presented breakfast with pleasant conversation and sweet memories.  We brought our bikes and took advantage of the rail trail and the nightlife of Napa.  I highly recommend this B&B as it is snuggled in the residential section of Napa and it's classic beauty gives you a taste of the past.  And for all those shy of the recent fires in the area... I want to assure you that this area is alive and well... as beautiful as it has always been.  I definitely recommend visiting!  Ask for the Carriage House... you will love the cozy robes... I promise you won't want to leave.</review>

<Review>Room was quite alright. Cleanliness is the major problem. Carpet was not clean. Bathroom was too small to turn your body around in there, even for a woman. Bed was comfortable, though. But in general they were quite stingy on the basic amenities provided in the room.

Breakfast was OK, I guess. Muffins, I was told, however, were quite good. We were given a big pot of coffee without being asked. And we don't drink coffee. That's a bummer.

There are nice rose bushes  in the garden.

Housekeepers (maids) really need to be improved.

Not quite satisfied with our stay. Would not come back.< /Review><pictures>None< /pictures>< Response>

The worst Staples I've ever been to.

I've been coming here for over 5 years because it's the closest one to me and there aren't many more in the area.

The store and bathrooms (which you now need the passkey for) are filthy and worst of all I think the employees move purposely slow -- especially at the Copy & Print Center.

Then when you get checked out, the transaction will take forever (because of both the cashiers dragging their feet and the delays with the computers).

< Text>
I have been bringing my motorcycle here for 5 years.  I have never had any problems with the employees.  My ride is always finished when they say it is going to be done. On 3-23-13 I brought my bike in due to a loud squeeking in the forks.  I advised the owner and his son Clint that I was just in less than 2 months ago for a tune-up and for all the front end bearings to be re-greased.  I told them that the noise started about a month after the service.  They told me not to worry that they would take care of it at no charge.  I left the bike there at 9:00 am and went back at 4:00 pm to my ride being fixed.  Turns out after the grease settled in the neck, it created some air pockets causing the squeek.  If you have ever had this service done you know it is expensive and takes all day.  No questions asked, even without knowing for sure what the issue was, they took care of it, on them.

Keep up the good work!< /Text>
